 The political journey of Narendra Modi
 
 
 -narendra modi kaa janm 17 sitambar, 1950 ko gujarat main mehsana ke vaadanagar main ek madhyamvargeey hindu parivaar main hua
 Modi's father's name is Domdar Moolchand Modi and mother's name is Hiraben Modi
 -bachapan main vah sadhu bananaa chaahate the
 Ran away from home to North India to become a monk
 kuch din saadhuon ke saath gujaarne ke baad modi ne sadhu banane kaa iraadaa tyaag diya or kuch saalon baad waapas laut aae
 Back home, he sold tea in Ahmedabad
 -modi ne gujarat uniwarsity se raajnneeti vigyaan main master degree praapt kii
 In 1987, Modi joined the Bharatiya Janata Party (BJP)
 us vakt bijepi ne hindu rashtrawaad ko lekar kaaphi jor pakad rahi thi
 After the BJP came to power in Gujarat in 1995, Modi's dominance increased
 -gujarat main bijepi kii neenv majboot karne main shankar singh waghela ke saath narendra modi kaa bhi naam shaamil he
 During college, he was an RSS pracharak, while Vaghela was a big gathering leader
 vahi din the jab modi main chhipi kaabiliyat ko pahachaanaa gaya
 His strategy was praised everywhere
 -lekin gujarat main modi or waghela kii ye jodi zyada dinon tak nahin chal saki
 After the BJP came to power in Gujarat in 1995, Modi was given the responsibility of two important visits
 unhen laalkrishna adwani kii somnath se lekar ayodhya tak kii rathyatra or kanyakumari se kashmir tak ke march kii yatra yojit karne kii jimmedaari saunpi gai
 In 1995, Modi was made the national secretary of the BJP and was given the responsibility of 5 states
 iske baad unhen mahasachiv banaaya gaya
 After this, he was given great responsibility in campaigning in Gujarat and Himachal
 -2001 main jab gujarat main bukamp ke aane se 20,000 log maare gaye tab rajya main raajnneetik satta main bhi badlaav hua
 Under pressure, the then Chief Minister Keshubhai Patel had to step down
 patel kii jagah narendra modi ko rajya kii kaman saunpi gai or iske baad modi ne kabhi peeche mudakar nahin dekha or vah aaj tak gujarat kii satta par damdaar tareek se kabiz hai
 After this, in the year 2002, not only Gujarat but a black chapter was added in the history of the whole country, which no one had thought about
 godhra main ek train main savaar 50 hinduon ke jalane ke baad puure gujarat main jo dange bhadke uskaa kalank modi aaj tak nahin dho paae hai

 maare gaye logon main adhikansh muslim the
 Modi was accused of inciting the riots

 -dangon main dhoomil hui chhavi ke baavjood varsh 2002 main hue vidhansabha chunaav main bhi modi kii jeet hui
 - In 2005, the US refused to grant a visa to Modi
 -2007 main vidhansabha chunaav main phir modi kii jeet hui or vah duusari baar rajya ke mukhyamantri bane
 In 2008, Modi invited Tata to open a Nano car plant
 ab tak gujarat bijli, sadak ke maamle main kaaphi viksit ho chukaa tha
 It was counted among the rich and developed states of the country
 modi ne adhik se adhik nivesh ko rajya main aamantrit kiya
 By 2012, Modi's stature in the BJP had grown so much that he was seen as the party's PM candidate
 -31 agast, 2012 ko modi ne online tareeke se vaib cam ke jariye janata ke sawaalon ke jawaab die

 -modi ne janata se judane ke liye twitor kaa istemaal kiya

 -22 oktober, 2012 ko british ucchayukta ne modi se milakar gujarat kii tarif kii or vahaan nivesh kiye jane kii baat kii
 With this, relations between Britain and Gujarat, which were disrupted after the riots, were restored
 -disambar, 2012 main modi ne chunaav prachaar ke dauraan thri-di technology kaa istemaal kiya or rajya kii zyada se zyada janata ko sambodhit kiya
